    var trackJsDeferred = (function() {
        var deferred = $.Deferred();

        function deferTrackJsCall(callee, args) {
            deferred.then(function() {
                window.trackJs[callee].apply(window.trackJs, args);
            });
        }

        function deferTrackJsConsoleCall(callee, args) {
            deferred.then(function() {
                window.trackJs.console[callee].apply(window.trackJs.console, args);
            });
        }

        if (window._trackJs.enabled && !window.trackJs) {
            window.trackJs = {
                console: {}
            };

            ['watchAll', 'watch', 'track'].forEach(function(callee) {
                window.trackJs[callee] = function() {
                    deferTrackJsCall(callee, arguments);
                }
            });

            ['debug', 'error', 'info', 'log', 'warn'].forEach(function(callee) {
                window.trackJs.console[callee] = function() {
                    deferTrackJsConsoleCall(callee, arguments);
                }
            });

            window.onerror = function(message, source, lineno, colno, error) {
                if (deferred.state() === 'pending') {
                    trackJs.track(error || message);
                }
            }

            var openAjax = XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open;
            XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open = function(method, url) {
                this.addEventListener('readystatechange', function() {
                    if (
                        deferred.state() === 'pending'
                        && this.readyState == XMLHttpRequest.DONE
                        && (this.status == 0 || this.status >= 400)
                    ) {
                        trackJs.track('[HTTP ' + this.status + '] ' + method + ': ' + url);
                    }
                });
                openAjax.apply(this, arguments);
            };

            window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection', function(e) {
                if (deferred.state() === 'pending') {
                    trackJs.track('Unhandled promise rejection due to {' + e.reason + '} Trace: ' + e.path);
                }
            });
        }

        return deferred;
    })();
</script>
<!-- END TRACKJS -->

    <script>
        (function() {
            if (!trackJsDeferred) console.warn('TrackJs dependency broken'); // Spot out breaking the dependency while in dev env
            if (!window._trackJs.enabled) return;
            var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
            xhr.open('GET', 'https://d2zah9y47r7bi2.cloudfront.net/releases/current/tracker.js');
            xhr.msCaching = 'enabled';
            xhr.addEventListener('load', function() {
                window.trackJs = null;
                eval(this.responseText);
                trackJsDeferred && trackJsDeferred.resolve();
            });
            xhr.send();
        })();
